### All languages

[be5invis / Iosevka](../../../../../be5invis/Iosevka)  
Spatial efficient monospace font family for programming. Built from code.  

[reactide / reactide](../../../../../reactide/reactide)  
Reactide is the first dedicated IDE for React web application development. http://reactide.io  

[freeCodeCamp / freeCodeCamp](../../../../../freeCodeCamp/freeCodeCamp)  
The https://freeCodeCamp.com open source codebase and curriculum. Learn to code and help nonprofits.  

[luanfujun / deep-photo-styletransfer](../../../../../luanfujun/deep-photo-styletransfer)  
Code and data for paper "Deep Photo Style Transfer": https://arxiv.org/abs/1703.07511  

[junyanz / CycleGAN](../../../../../junyanz/CycleGAN)  
Software that generates photos from paintings, turns horses into zebras, performs style transfer, and more (from UC Berkeley)  

[toddmotto / public-apis](../../../../../toddmotto/public-apis)  
A collective list of public JSON APIs for use in web development.  

[huntergregal / mimipenguin](../../../../../huntergregal/mimipenguin)  
A tool to dump the login password from the current linux user  

[Idnan / bash-guide](../../../../../Idnan/bash-guide)  
A guide to learn bash  

[kamranahmedse / developer-roadmap](../../../../../kamranahmedse/developer-roadmap)  
Roadmap to becoming a web developer in 2017  

[jwasham / coding-interview-university](../../../../../jwasham/coding-interview-university)  
A complete computer science study plan to become a software engineer.  

[oneuijs / You-Dont-Need-jQuery](../../../../../oneuijs/You-Dont-Need-jQuery)  
Examples of how to do query, style, dom, ajax, event etc like jQuery with plain javascript.  

[matcornic / hermes](../../../../../matcornic/hermes)  
Golang package that generates clean, responsive HTML e-mails for sending transactional mail  

[getify / You-Dont-Know-JS](../../../../../getify/You-Dont-Know-JS)  
A book series on JavaScript. @YDKJS on twitter.  

[vhf / free-programming-books](../../../../../vhf/free-programming-books)  
üìö Freely available programming books  

[vasanthk / react-bits](../../../../../vasanthk/react-bits)  
‚ú® React patterns, techniques, tips and tricks ‚ú®  

[vinta / awesome-python](../../../../../vinta/awesome-python)  
A curated list of awesome Python frameworks, libraries, software and resources  

[EyreFree / EFQRCode](../../../../../EyreFree/EFQRCode)  
A better way to operate two-dimensional code in Swift.  

[bmorelli25 / Become-A-Full-Stack-Web-Developer](../../../../../bmorelli25/Become-A-Full-Stack-Web-Developer)  
Free resources for learning Full Stack Web Development  

[jevakallio / redux-offline](../../../../../jevakallio/redux-offline)  
Build Offline-First Apps for Web and React Native  

[jlund / streisand](../../../../../jlund/streisand)  
Streisand sets up a new server running L2TP/IPsec, OpenConnect, OpenSSH, OpenVPN, Shadowsocks, sslh, Stunnel, a Tor bridge, and WireGuard. It also generates custom instructions for all of these services. At the end of the run you are given an HTML file with instructions that can be shared with friends, family members, and fellow activists.  

[atlassian / localstack](../../../../../atlassian/localstack)  
A fully functional local AWS cloud stack. Develop and test your cloud apps offline!  

[donnemartin / system-design-primer](../../../../../donnemartin/system-design-primer)  
Learn how to design large-scale systems. Prep for the system design interview.  

[tensorflow / tensorflow](../../../../../tensorflow/tensorflow)  
Computation using data flow graphs for scalable machine learning  

[bharathgs / Awesome-pytorch-list](../../../../../bharathgs/Awesome-pytorch-list)  
A comprehensive list of pytorch related content on github,such as different models,implementations,helper libraries,tutorials etc.  

[vuejs / vue](../../../../../vuejs/vue)  
A progressive, incrementally-adoptable JavaScript framework for building UI on the web.

An ActionScript 3 Library that contains a number of classes and utilities for working with ActionScript? 3. These include classes for MD5 and SHA 1 hashing, Image encoders, and JSON serialization as well as general String, Number and Date APIs.

flixel is a free Actionscript (Flash) library that I distilled from a variety of Flash games that I've worked on over the last couple years, including Gravity Hook, Fathom and Canabalt. It's primary function is to provide some useful base classes that you can extend to make your own game objects.

### Ada

[cforler / Ada-Crypto-Library](../../../../../cforler/Ada-Crypto-Library)  
The libadacrypt-dev is a crypto library for Ada with a nice API. It is written for the i386 and x86_64 hardware architecture and supports AES, Twofish, 3DES, Serpent SHA-1/256/384/512, DSA, OAEP-RSA, HMAC, CMAC, SIV, OCB, Nonces, Elliptic Curves. etc. It also contains regression tests consisting of over 400 tests. Dependencies: make and gnat-4.9.

[frkunz / stELMOD](../../../../../frkunz/stELMOD)  
stELMOD is a stochastic optimization model to analyze the impact of uncertain wind generation on the dayahead and intraday electricity markets as well as network congestion management. The consecutive clearing of the electricity markets is incorporated by a rolling planning procedure resembling the market process of most European markets.
